0(): 'arganganan mnananan nar nan/ rnam na/
1(): pU ra k+Sha ra ba dzA yA na
2(): se na ra d+hA pu
3(): ba/ dz+wa yA/ na ta n+yA se na ra t+yA du/ ste/ kA/ ste/
4(): snga 'gyur rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud sde rin po che'i glegs pa ma bzhugs so//
1a1(1): bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa thams cad kyi snying po rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod rdo rje theg pa snga
1a2(1): 'drar rgyang 'phrus zing ba che'i tshogs pa brjod pa sa ri po can bu'i gtam zhes bya ba'i sang cha bzhugs so//
1b1(1): de la bong 'dir dpal gsang ba'i snying po'i bshad pa'i chu 'go lta bur gyur pa gsang bdag sgo phug pa chen po'am
1b2(1): zur shAkya seng ge ni/ jo sras mo mda' mo gtsug tor lcam zhes bya ba slob mar gyur pa zhig yod pa des mngal du sprul pa'i sku 'dzin
1b3(1): nus par dgongs nas/ de nyid kyi ming po ka ba bzhi'i gras mnga' tig chos shAkya la/ khyod kyi sring mo 'di bdag gir rung ngam zhes
1b4(1): gsungs pas/ mda' tig na re/ bka' bzhin 'tshal zhes de'i lag pa na rdo rje dril bu bzhag ste/ 'di gzhan la ma brgyud par
2a1(1): bla ma'i phrag tu phul zhig par bsgos pas rten 'brel chen po 'grigs/ de khab tu bzhes pa ma yin pas gra ba'i
2a2(1): tshogs kyang sdang zhing 'don par brtsams pa na/ skyo ston shA ka ye na re/ 'di'i srin lag la bstan pa'i gtso bo gcig 'dug
2a3(1): par rmis pas/ rigs sras 'dra mthong na bstan par phan srid kyi zhog gsungs/ de bzhin du ka ba gzhan rnams la 'ang
2a4(1): sangs rgyas kyi sku dang / gser gyi rdo rje sogs jo mo la thim par rmis pas bzhag go// de la rdog lo chen po'i bcu drug
2b1(1): pa shing pho stag la sgro phug pa slu bltams/ der bla ma'i zhal nas nga'i bu 'di lhums su 'jug pa'i tshe phyag na rdo rje thim pa'i mtshan ma yod pa yin pas 'gro ba la phan pa//
2b2(1): zhig yod gsungs nas/ mtshan shAkya seng ger btags/ yab kyis spong dag byas nas ci yang med pa dang thug pas/ yum na re/ kha sing nas bu skye ba ni thugs
2b3(1): la mnga'/ rkan mar tsam yang mi 'jog pa zer ba la/ kho la bsod nams yod na ngas ma bzhag kyang 'ong / de med na bzhag kyang mi phan gsungs khang thog na bzhugs
2b4(1): tsa na/ btsun ma phyug mo zhig gis nas rgyab mang po dang / mar phon cher phul/ mdo khams nas 'bul skyes lhags pas/ 'di la bsod nams kyang 'ong / 'gro
2b5(1): pa lang phan gsungs/ zla ba brgyad na yab gshegs pas/ yum dang zhang pos bskyangs nas mnga' phur lo bco lnga bzhugs/ de nas chu bar du gla na shAkya bzang
2b6(1): po'i drung du byon nas gsang ba sgyu 'phrul dang / skyo lung du yang khyed gi sar yang byon nas chos gsan/ dgung lo bcu dgu pa la che 'don mdzad pas phrin las shin tu rgyas te/
3a1(1): bslab gcer g.yol ba byung / der skabs bsal nas gong bur bu'i rtsar la gcig zin/ de nas slar phrin las cher rgyas te gzhan du bzhud paH/
3a2(1): skabs ma byung / bla ma mkhas grub kyi tshogs tshur spyan drangs nas slob gnyer rdzogs par mdzad/ khyad par ka ba bzhi las yab chos mdo sgyu sems gsum rgyud
3a3(1): man ngag phrin sgrub phyag ba zhes dbang dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan cing khyad par du zhang po mda' tig las mdo'i skor zhib par brnyes//
3a4(1): glan shAkya byang chub la rdzogs chen skor lugs/ lha rje shangs nag la rdzogs chen brgyad pa tha ma sog mdor na bla ma mang po la thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs chod par//
3a5(1): par mdzad// rang gi grub mtha' gsan pa'i bla ma de dag la'ang yum rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyis sna drangs pa'i 'bul ba rgya chen pos thugs zin par mdzad//
3a6(1): nya ri sgro phug tu sgrub pa yun ring mdzad pas bskyed rdzogs kyi gnas la man ngag gi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i gzer bzhi thebs/ yi dam lha'i sku gsung thugs dang tha
3b1(1): dad med par 'dres pa'i sku gzhon nu nas gzi byin shin tu che ste thams cad zil gyis gnon nus/ re zhig na dam pa sangs rgyas dang rin bzhugs pa dpon slob lngas mjal du byon/
3b2(1): phebs rgyu'i nyin dam pa'i zhal nas de ring phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa 'byon pa yod kyi bsu bgyis gsungs/ dar gdugs la sogs bshams pas/ nyi ma rgas su chas tsa na sngan
3b3(1): pa dpon slob lnga byung / gzhan su yang mi mda' zhus pas/ de ka la bsu bgyis gsungs/ der lha rje spro phrag pas dam pa la mngon mkhyen me 'dug blta yi gsungs nas
3b4(1): slob ma zhig nyid du brdzur bcug nas sngon la gtang // khong rang phrin zhabs 'bring ba ltar byas pas/ dam pas spro ba'i mgul na lba ba yod pa la gzigs nas/ phyag na lba ba can
3b5(1): gyis drongs/ dpon slob go ma log pa bzang gsungs pas/ mos gus chen po thob/ chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang nod/ dam pa'i zhal nas sgro phug pa la 'di bstan pa'i spyi dpal
3b6(1): chen por 'gyur zhes dbugs 'byin mdzad/ yang re zhig na phyag rdor gyi bris sku byed pa'i bri bkod kyi tshe/ lha bris pa la khyed rang 'di 'dra ba zhig bris zhes phyag na rdo
4a1(1): rje'i skur dngos su bstan pa sogs rgya mtshan du ma'i sgo nas dpal gsang ba'i bdag po byang phyogs kyi rgyud 'dir gsang sngags kyi bstan pa
4a2(1): rgyas par mdzad pa la byon no zhes grags/ spyir gdul bu'i tshogs dpag tu med la/ khyad par slob ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po grus 'dzin cing bstan pa
4a3(1): skyong ba gdugs thogs pa stong thon pas ri mo'i mthar yang phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab/ sgo phug tu chos gsungs pa'i dus gcig chos khri rgyab yos med pa
4a4(1): gcig la bzhugs te mtha' skor thams cad gra pas bskor nas yod pa la/ phyogs thams cad du zhal thal le bar byung bas rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i
4a5(1): dkyil 'khor gyi bdag po'i zhal sbyin mngon sum par yid ches shing sbrul sgur rtsod pa med par grags/ dbyar chos dgun chos kyi dus phyogs ren mar dpe
4a6(1): 'grims lnga brgya tsam re dang / ston chos dang dpyid chos kyis sum brgya tsam yod cing / spyir khri khrag thal ba byung bas/ chos ra'i go sa bde dog
4b1(1): la'ang gser zho re'i 'jal len byed pa'i dar rgyas byung / mkhyen brtse nus gsum gyi yon tan phun tshogs shing dpal gsang ba'i snying po de kho na
4b2(1): nyid nges pa'i rgyud don la rang byan tshud pa tsam gyis chos spyan thob pas gsang bdag sgro phug pa'i bshad srol zhes dus da lta'i bar du lnga pa ljib byed
4b3(1): pa 'di byung zhing nyi zla ltar grags pa yin no// de la thugs zin gyi slob ma bcu gnyis byung ste/ nag po bzhi/ ston pa bzhi/ mes
4b4(1): bzhi las/ nag po bzhi ni/ lce ston rgyan ga/ zur nag 'khor lo// nyang nag mdo bo/ mda' nag gtsug tor dbang phyug go//
4b5(1): ston pa bzhi ni/ nyi ston chos ser/ rgyabs ston rdo rje mgon po// zhang ston/ rgya ston bzhi'o// me sa bzhi ni/ rtsangs pa byi
4b6(1): ston/ g.yu ston hor po// spangs ston lcags kyu/ dbus pa chos seng ngo // 'dron tshul 'di zur stod lugs su grags la/ smad
5a1(1): lugs su de las tha dad pa' nga yod/ de ltar sprul pa'i sku ka sang ba dag spro phug pa chen po de nyid tha ma'i mdzad pa ston
5a2(1): par babs pa'i tshe/ ston pa bzhi la khyod chos tshogs 'khor gyi cha rkyen 'dra khyer la shog/ ngas kyang sngogs kyi gsungs/ ston pa bzhis gsung
5a3(1): bzhin du bsgrubs pa dang / sgro phug gi ltag lha ri gdong gi rtser byon nas tshogs 'khor rgya chen po mdzad/ gsung gi gsang ba mang po rjes su bstan
5a4(1): nas/ khyod rnamasar med pa la mya ngan ma byed cig/ ngas da res lus ma spangs par khyer nas rig 'dzin gyi sa la 'gro ba yin/ des khyed rnams
5a5(1): la shul du'ang bkra shis/ mi rgyud dang bstan pa 'phel ba gcig 'ong ngo gsungs nas/ dpal gyi mgur las rdo rje'i glu gcig bzhengs/
5a6(1): nam mkha' la je mtho je mthor 'phags kyi na mgur re bzhe sa nas mthar mi mngon pa'i sar gshegs pa dang / ston pa bzhi snying phyung ba lta bu'i
5b1(1): sdug bsngal gyis mnar nas cho nges ba ta ba/ 'gre ldog byas/ mtshan nas bos pas bya ba bas pa bzhin du byon/ khyed rnams de ltar mi byed pa
5b2(1): yin te/ ngas gong du kha ta ni legs par bcug/ de la mi nyan par/ da nga'i mi rgyud la bkra shis pa ba ga mi 'ong gsungs/ de nas phyi lo drug
5b3(1): cu rtsa gcig pa shing pho stag la 'ong min tshogs chen 'dus pa'i grong khyer du gshegs so// pur sbyong ba'i tshe sngags pa gzhon ma dze sa gcig gis rta dang
5b4(1): bzang gcig la dung gi sga rang gug ngo mtshar can bstad pa zhig phul/ de 'di nas byung dang 'dir song sus kyang ngo shes pa ma byung bas lhas 'degs
5b5(1): ba skyal bar grags/ de bzhin du btsan dang / ma mo dang / klu rnams kyis kyang 'degs bskyal te/ mi la med pa'i nor sna bzhi byung ba yin/
5b6(1): no// 'dis skye ba kun dga' snying po las lo bco brgyad kyis bgres pas dwags po lha rje dang / phag mo grung / bla ma zhang / jo sras
6a1(1): 'dzed sogs dang thog rags pa tsam mnyam mo// yang bi ma la'i slob ma rong chu tshan gyi dge slong ma spre mo// de'i
6a2(1): slob ma lho brag bya ze'i mar pa shes rab 'od/ de'i slo ba ma shangs lha bu'i lang ston dar ma bsod nams/ de'i slob ma lha rje hor po sgo phug pa yin
6a3(1): pas bi ma la dang gnyis kyi bar la bla ma gsum las med do// // de la sgro phug pa'i slob ma lce ston rgya nag ni 'khrungs nyang stod pa yin/ mtshan
6a4(1): nyid kyi grwa sa na phu bo gnyis slob gnyer la yod pa'i sar rgyags skyel du byon/ zhar nyan byas pas khong gnyis kyis ched du sbyangs pa las lhag pa byung //
6a5(1): der rgyan ga na re// khyed gnyis kyis lo gsum nyan kyang go ba ci yang mi 'dug/ ngas nyan na go ba 'dug byas pas/ phu bo gnyis na re/ nged
6a6(1): gnyis la de las ma byung / chos sus shes kyang 'dra yi khyod go na khyod rang nyon/ ded kyis rgyags skyel byed zer bas/ der lha rje rgyan ga
6b1(1): gis bzhugs nas khyung po grags sel phar phyin/ 'ban la mngon pa/ stag pa kha che la dbu tshad/ 'gar bsod nams ye shes la'
6b2(1): gtugs te lo dgur nyan pas mkhas pa'i pha rol tu son/ sum cu pa'i tshe gsang ba dag sgro phug pa la sngags ga san du byon na sa lo bcu gcig
6b3(1): bzhugs te/ lo gsum gyi bar jo sra sa nyang stod pa ga su ngas pa tsam las spyan sngar gsung gleng zhi ba pa tsam ma byung skabs shi ka na rgya brtson seng
6b4(1): dpon g.yog dang lha rje chos 'khor sta bas gcig tu 'joms pa'i tshe/ rgya brtson dpon g.yog gis rtsod pa btsugs pas/ lha rje rgyan ga
6b5(1): gis khong rnams sun phyung / nga rgyal bcag pas mnyes te thugs la 'dogs par byung ba'i khar/ sra sa jo btsun rdo rje grags blo kha phye bas
6b6(1): rab tu dgyes nas/ bskyed rdzogs gsum gyi gzhung gdams ngag dang / khyad par gyi man ngag yig chung dang bcas pa gnang ba sa lha rje lha
7a1(1): khang pa zur tsho gzhan las chos kha tshang zhing man ngag za ba pa yin/ bzhi bcu tham pa la gshegs btsun mdzad//
7a2(1): de'i phyi lo sgro phug pa gshegs/ nyang stod kyi rgya tsang skor la bdud rtsi/ nyang smad sgro dar ser la rnam 'joms dang / phur pa rtsa ba sor
7a3(1): bzhag lugs/ gzhan yang skyi lugs la sogs phur pa lugs tha dad pa dang / dam pa spor mngal rdzogs chen spor lugs/ jo mo nyad
7a4(1): mo la rdzogs chen khams lugs a ro'i thugs bcud/ de bzhin du rdzogs chen bram ze'i skor dang ke tshang ma la sogs thos pa shin tu mang bas
7a5(1): sngags dang / mtshan nyid/ rgyud dang sgrub thabs thams cad kyi bdag por gyur/ sman sgrub mdzad pa'i tshe sman gyi pho brang las lha mo
7a6(1): mngon sum du thon nas dkyil 'khor la bskor ba lan gsum byas te thim par kun gyis mthong / gzhan don rgya chen po mdzad nas lnga bcu rtsa drug
7b1(1): pa la gshegs so// 'di'i dpon po bla ma chen po yon tan gzungs ni/ me po rta la 'khrungs/ bcu gcig nas slob gnyer mdzad//
7b2(1): lo bcu gsum khu bo dang 'grogs nas bskyed rdzogs gsum gyi rgyud lung man ngag kun la slo ba gnyer rdzogs/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi ba zhes pa'i tshe khu boH
7b3(1): nag pa sku gshegs nas gdan sa mdzad/ dbus pa ston shA ka dang / dbus pa zhig po sogs las the tshom gyi dras thams cad nas rang gzhan gyi/
7b4(1): don mdzad pa yin no// // dbus pa ston shA ka gam dam pa se skrag pa ni/ gzad kyi gcer pa wang thung rgyud yin/ sgro phug pa'i gra sar yi ge
7b5(1): 'drir byon pa la dad pa tho ba nas slob gnyer byas/ lha rje rgyan ga gshegs btsun mdzad pa'i phyir 'breng du gshegs nas rgyud dang ga dam sa ngag thams
7b6(1): cad rdzogs/ sgom sgrub 'ba' zhig bya bar bsams te bya nga ring dgon pa 'tshol du byon pas/ yol ba brag la dam pa yol chung ba brag brko ba
8a1(1): dang mjal/ 'dir dgon pa mdzad pa lags sam byas pa yin zer/ 'di min pa byas mi gda' 'am byas pas/
8a2(1): pha ngos na se ba kha brag can gcig na 'dug ste/ de bas 'di btsan pas 'dir byed zer/ der dam pa ston shA ka gis brag se ba kha skrag skyes pa der byon
8a3(1): tsan/ chu mig 'gram nas zan rdog 'ga' zhig rnyed pas bzang ltas su bzung / der bzhugs te sgom sgrub mdzad pas rtogs pa khyad par can skyes/
8a4(1): lha 'dres bka' la nyan kadul bya mang po'i don nus pa byung ste dam pa se skrag pa zhes grags so// // dbus pa zhig po ni/ yar klung byas pa yin/
8a5(1): rje sgro phug pa'i gdan sar yig mkhan chos la tshud pa zhig ste/ lha rje rgyanag gi phyi la 'brangs/ bskyed rdzogs gsum ka la 'byongs par byas/
8a6(1): yul la che 'don la 'gro snyam tsa na/ de'i cha rkyen gdugs dang / dung dang / mchod cha sogs dgos par sems nas de dag 'don pa'i phyir bal
8b1(1): yul du byon/ lam du bsam pa la ngas chos de tsam shes kyang nyams su blang rgyu zhig mi 'dug/ da lta shi na chis kyang mi phan/ gdams
8b2(1): ngag kho na la blo gtod dgongs par 'dug snyam nas slar log/ bla ma'i spyan sngar phyin nas zhus pas/ snyan pa rgyud rin po che'i gdams ngag
8b3(1): gnang / de la nyams len mdzad cing byon pas/ mang yul gung thang du rtol tsan rdzogs pa chen po'i ye shes brjod du med pa zhag bdun du
8b4(1): shar/ der bal po nas mchod cha blangs/ mang yul gung thang du lhogs tsam na/ tshad pa byin 'brangs nas bsnyungs/ da mi dga' ba
8b5(1): e yin snyam nas blo thag bcad/ ka tsa rnams grong du bzhag/ ri la byon nas nyams su blangs pas sa rdo ri brag thams cad la thogs pa med
8b6(1): pa byang / sngar gyi bsams pa de dag dgos me 'ga' zhig tu shes nas che 'don gyi ka ca thams cad gang dgar bsgyur/ many+dzi dang ting
9a1(1): bdun cha gcig yod pa de mthong ba dang bla ma'i drin dran te/ ngal dgongs pa 'di 'dra 'char ba yang bla ma'i thugs rje
9a2(1): yin pas 'di tsam zhig bla ma la 'bul dgos snyam khyer phyin pas/ 'dod pa zad pas de yang lam du bsgyur 'dod pa byung ste/ yang bla ma'i drin bsams
9a3(1): te byon/ lha khang du slebs tsan/ bla ma'i drung du bsgyur nas/ ting khyod kyis nga ji tsam zhig bcings gsung skad/ der ri 'ba' zhig la
9a4(1): bzhugs nas nyams len mdzad pas/ chos thams cad blo la 'char ba dang / snang ba bden med du bun long song ba sarba ba kyi sa ma tshugs//
9a5(1): g.ya sa ru'i ba gor phur bzhugs pa'i tshe gzims mal gyi steng du thog byung yang ma gnod/ gzhan gyis thog byung ngam zhus pas/ thog gam
9a6(1): de byung gsungs/ ma gnod dam zhus pas/ sgra zag stong dbyer med yin/ thog la rang bzhin ga la yod gsungs te rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug
9b1(1): chen por bzhugs/ sgom sgrub 'ba' zhig gi ngang nas mtshams 'og tu gra sa lo bco brgyad pa sbyangs/ dgung lo ba dun cu pa la gshegs so//
9b2(1): dam pa'i skyes bu 'di la slob ma/ zhig po bdud rtsi/ ston pa bla skya bas/ dbus pa jo ba sod/ snying ston nyi ma rdo rje la sogs pa gzhung
9b3(1): lugs la mkhas pa mang du byung / gzhan yang la stod kyi mes ston mgon po dang / dpyal kun dga' rdo rje la sogs pas kyang zhab sa la
9b4(1): gtugs so// // thugs kyi sras zhig po bdud rtsi ni/ ya ba mes kyi ring nas mkhas pa dang / grub pa'i dpa' bo brgyud mar byung ba
9b5(1): las 'di'i yab sangs rgyas dwags chung ste/ dwags po rgya ras kyi phyin 'brangs pa sa dwag sa chung bar gra ga sa/ des lho brag tu byon nas/ lho
9b6(1): stod phur mo nga skang bya ba'i dgon par 'gro don mdzad cing bzhugs pa la/ gzad pa'i yon pa dag rnams kyis gdan drangs/ gzad kyi lha gdong
10a1(1): @#dgon pa dang / 'ug skad dgon pa la sogs pa phul nas bzhugs/ bu slob mang du 'phel/ de la jo mo
10a2(1): war mo bya ba zhig yod pa dang gnyis kyi bur gzad kyi lha gdong dgon par btsas/ zhi ba ma'i nang du bskyal ba la 'ja' tshon zug/ dgung lo gnyis
10a3(1): tsam lon pa'i tshe ya ba la rmi lam ngo mtshar ba byung nas/ dang 'chi bar 'dug/ shi nas kyang rig 'dzin gyi sa la 'gro bar 'dug/ bu 'dis kyang
10a4(1): gzhan la phan thogs par 'dug gsungs te gshegs/ zhig po rin po 'di cher skyes pa dang snying rje shin tu che bas go sa bcos pa thams cad mas
10a5(1): ba shol kyang ma nyan par lam zan pa nyam thag gcig yod pa la byin/ der mo ma rnon po gcig na re/ khyod kyi bu 'di ci 'dra zhig 'ong / 'di la
10a6(1): 'jig rten gyi lha 'dre thams cad tshogs nas bskor ba byed cing mchod par 'dug zer/ ston ka gcig 'ongs 'don tsan/ mo na re/ mi thams
10b1(1): cad 'ongs 'don pa la gtor ma gtong gi 'dug/ glen pa khyod kyang chug tor 'dra thong / rang re yang 'ongs 'don pa yin byas pas/ 'ongs
10b2(1): 'don sar byis pa des song nas/ gzad lung pa'i lha 'dre tsho/ nyang nag 'ol po'i lha 'dre tsho/ sprang po'u lu'i rgyal nag/ da nang su'i yang
10b3(1): sar ma 'gro bar/ rgan mo wang mo'i 'ongs 'don gyi yod pas 'di'i 'ongs la sa khyer zer nas/ thor thor byas pas/ a ma khros nas
10b4(1): phyar gyin 'dug/ der zhing re bzhi bya ba lo nan ltar legs na'ang bzhi bcu las mi thon pa zhig la/ de'i lo skye ma ha cang med pa la khal lnga
10b5(1): bcu thal ba byung ba sa 'di sprul pa gcig yin nyen 'jug zer nas/ zhang po dam pa se smug pa'i rtswa ra slob gnyer la ba tang / lo gsum
10b6(1): gyi ring la rdzogs chen rong lugs/ sgang dril/ gab phyur sogs legs par thos/ bla ma gshegs khar mig mchi ma sa 'gags
11a1(1): #nas dran pa tsam ma byung gsungs/ bcu drug pa la skyil mkhar lha khang pa yon tan gzungs kyi zhab sa la
11a2(1): gtugs/ lo mang du bzhugs nas bskyed rdzogs gsum ka la blo gros byang bar mdzad/ nyams len gyi gtso bo dang 'chad nyan thams cad sems phyogs la
11a3(1): mdzad de zhal gyis kyang sems phyogs kho na bsgrubs pa yin gsungs/ kun byed rgyal po dang mdo bcu la sogs pa sems phyogs kyi rgyud sde chen po nyi shu rtsa bzhi
11a4(1): kas na/ rtsa ba sems sde'i skor la/ skor lugs rang lugs/ khams lugs la sogs pa bshad srol mi gcig pa bcu bzhig sa na/ rang
11a5(1): lugs kyi sgom yig chen po rnams las/ rnal 'byor rig pa'i nyi ma/ bsam gtan mig gi sgron ma/ bsam gtan snying gi nyi ma/ ka dar
11a6(1): sha dang gzer bu/ zhu len khung gdag/ rdo rje sems dpa'i zhu lan sogs sgom yig phal mo che thos/ snyan brgyud kyi skor la/ skor rong
11b1(1): khams gsum ka'i gdams pa dang / bram ze'i skor gyi snyan brgyud/ ke tshang dang / rdzogs phrang snyan brgyud krong la sogs pa bsam gyis mi
11b2(1): khyab pa zhig ga san te/ rdzogs chen gyi skor la thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs lhag par chod pa yin/ dgung lo bcu drug la bshar pa mdzad re skor
11b3(1): lugs kyi stong thun gsungs pas mkhas pa'i thog chod/ der lha rje gnub sa sman bya ba na re/ dbus pa'i jo sras khyed nga'i rta khyung phrug kha che dang 'dra
11b4(1): ba 'dug zor/ nas khal bcu gcig gi phyogs byas skad/ bla ma lha khang pa'i drung du lo bcu bzhi bzhugs/ bar skabs kun tu zhang po'i
11b5(1): gdan sa se skrag tu'ang bzhugs te sgom sgrub dang bshad pa bag re mdzad/ slob gnyer tshar ba dang yab kyi slob ma bla ma mdos bya ba gcig gis
